add_namespace = alash


country_event = {
	id = alash.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.1" }
	title = alash.1.t
	desc = alash.1.d
	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_ALO_alash
	option = {
		name = alash.1.a
		country_event = {
			id = alash.899
			days = 1
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = alash.1002
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.1002" }
	immediate = { 
		hidden_effect = { 
			clr_country_flag = ALO_elections_ongoing		
			ALO_run_election = yes
			set_country_flag = { flag = ALO_show_deputies_comparison value = 1 days = 30 }
			set_variable = { ALO_total_deputies = ALO_ush_zhus_deputies }
			add_to_variable = { ALO_total_deputies = ALO_zhas_azamat_deputies }
			add_to_variable = { ALO_total_deputies = ALO_azat_deputies }
			add_to_variable = { ALO_total_deputies = ALO_zhanar_deputies }
			add_to_variable = { ALO_total_deputies = ALO_alash_deputies }
			add_to_variable = { ALO_total_deputies = ALO_national_deputies }
			add_to_variable = { ALO_total_deputies = ALO_cossack_deputies }
			add_to_variable = { ALO_total_deputies = ALO_russian_deputies }			
			ALO_calculate_support = yes
		} 
	}
	title = alash.1000.t
	desc = alash.1000.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = ALO_empowered_president
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = ALO_political_crisis
			has_war_with = var:219.owner
		}		
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_ALO_parliament

	option = {
		name = alash.1000.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = ALO_ELECTION_USH_ZHUS_VICTORY }
	}
	option = {
		name = alash.1000.b
		trigger = { has_country_flag = ALO_ELECTION_ZHAS_AZAMAT_VICTORY }		
	}
	option = {
		name = alash.1000.c
		trigger = { 
			has_country_flag = ALO_ELECTION_AZAT_VICTORY 
			ALO_alash_left_independent = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = alash.1000.e
		trigger = { has_country_flag = ALO_ELECTION_ZHANAR_VICTORY }
	}
	option = {
		name = alash.1000.f
		trigger = { 
			has_country_flag = ALO_ELECTION_ALASH_VICTORY 
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = alash.1000.g
		trigger = { 
			has_country_flag = ALO_ELECTION_NATIONAL_VICTORY
		}
	}	
}
country_event = {

	desc = alash.1001.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

		has_war_with = var:219.owner
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_ALO_parliament

	option = {
		name = alash.1001.a
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = var:current_party_ideology_group
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 12
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = alash.1000
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.1000" }
	immediate = { 
		hidden_effect = { 
			clr_country_flag = ALO_elections_ongoing		
			ALO_run_election = yes
			set_country_flag = { flag = ALO_show_deputies_comparison value = 1 days = 30 }
			set_variable = { ALO_total_deputies = ALO_ush_zhus_deputies }
			add_to_variable = { ALO_total_deputies = ALO_zhas_azamat_deputies }
			add_to_variable = { ALO_total_deputies = ALO_azat_deputies }
			add_to_variable = { ALO_total_deputies = ALO_zhanar_deputies }
			add_to_variable = { ALO_total_deputies = ALO_alash_deputies }
			add_to_variable = { ALO_total_deputies = ALO_national_deputies }
			add_to_variable = { ALO_total_deputies = ALO_cossack_deputies }
			add_to_variable = { ALO_total_deputies = ALO_russian_deputies }			
			ALO_calculate_support = yes
			
			country_event = { id = alash.1003 months = 56 }
		} 
	}
	title = alash.1000.t
	desc = alash.1000.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = ALO_political_crisis
			has_country_flag = ALO_empowered_president
			has_war_with = var:219.owner
		}		
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_ALO_parliament

	option = {
		name = alash.1000.a
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = ALO_ELECTION_USH_ZHUS_VICTORY 
				AND = {
					is_ai = yes
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = ALO_path option = ALO_PATH_USH_JUS }
						has_game_rule = { rule = ALO_path option = ALO_PATH_USH_JUS_PANTURKIST }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = radical_socialist
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 60
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			ALO_Muqan_Aitpenov_hog_rso
			ALO_Uzaqbay_Qulymbetov_for_rso
			ALO_Torsanov_Qaziy_eco_rso
			ALO_Abilkair_Dosov_sec_rso
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = ALO_natpops_part_of_ush_jus }
			add_natpop_to_coalition = yes
		}
		set_variable = { ALO_ush_zhus_deputies_support = ALO_ush_zhus_deputies }
		ALO_calculate_support = yes
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = ALO_Ush_Jus_Victory }
			}
			complete_national_focus = ALO_Ush_Jus_Victory
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = alash.1000.b
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = ALO_ELECTION_ZHAS_AZAMAT_VICTORY 
				AND = {
					is_ai = yes
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = ALO_path option = ALO_PATH_SOCDEM }
						has_game_rule = { rule = ALO_path option = ALO_PATH_SOCDEM_DEM }
						has_game_rule = { rule = ALO_path option = ALO_PATH_SOCDEM_LIB }
					}
				}
			}
		}		
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_democrat
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 60
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes		
		add_ideas = {
			ALO_Smagul_Sadvakasov_hog_sde
			ALO_Omar_Almasov_for_sde
			ALO_Jusupbek_Aymautov_eco_sde
			ALO_Muhtar_Auezov_sec_sde
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Smagul Säduaqasov"
			desc = "POLITICS_SMAGUL_SADUAQASOV_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/ALO/Portrait_ALO_Smagul_Saduakasov.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = socdem_radical_progressivism_subtype 
		}
		set_variable = { ALO_zhas_azamat_deputies_support = ALO_zhas_azamat_deputies }		
		ALO_calculate_support = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = ALO_birlik_established }
			add_synd_to_coalition = yes
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ALO_birlik_established_mynbayev }
				remove_ideas_with_trait = security_minister
				add_ideas = ALO_Jalau_Mynbayev_sec_syn
			}
		}
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = ALO_Zhas_Azamat_Victory }
			}
			complete_national_focus = ALO_Zhas_Azamat_Victory
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = alash.1000.c
		trigger = { 
			has_country_flag = ALO_ELECTION_AZAT_VICTORY 
			ALO_alash_left_independent = yes
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_democrat
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 60
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes		
		add_ideas = {
			ALO_Zhahansha_Dosmukhamedov_hog_sde
			ALO_Khalel_Dosmuhamedov_for_sli
			ALO_Alpysypay_Kalmenev_eco_sli
			ALO_Dauletshe_Kusepkaliev_sec_sli
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Jahansha Dosmukhamedov"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/ALO/Portrait_ALO_Zhakhansha_Dosmukhammedov.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = socdem_left_nationalism_subtype
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			name = ALO_socdem_party
			long_name = ALO_socdem_party_long
		}
		set_variable = { ALO_azat_deputies_support = ALO_azat_deputies }
		ALO_calculate_support = yes
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = alash.1000.e
		trigger = {  
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = ALO_ELECTION_ZHANAR_VICTORY 
				AND = {
					is_ai = yes

				}
			}
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_liberal

					election_frequency = 60
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}

		add_ideas = {
			ALO_Mirzhakip_Dulatov_hog_sli
			ALO_Ahmet_Beremzhanov_for_sli
			ALO_Khalel_Gabbasov_eco_sli
			ALO_Bazarbay_Mametov_sec_sli
		}
		set_variable = { ALO_zhanar_deputies_support = ALO_zhanar_deputies }
		ALO_calculate_support = yes

		if = {

	}

		trigger = {

				has_country_flag = ALO_ELECTION_ALASH_VICTORY

			}
		}

country_event = {
	id = alash.1003
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.1003" }
	title = alash.1003.t
	desc = alash.1003.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_elections = yes
		NOT = { has_war_with = var:219.owner }
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_ALO_parliament
	
	option = {
		name = alash.1003.a
		set_country_flag = ALO_elections_ongoing
		if = {
			limit = { 
				ALO_ush_juz_in_power = no
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ush_zhus_banned }
			}
			activate_mission = ALO_ush_zhus_campaign
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				ALO_jas_azamat_in_power = no
				NOT = { has_country_flag = zhas_azamat_banned }
			}
			activate_mission = ALO_zhas_azamat_campaign
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				ALO_alash_party_in_power = no				
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_reorganized }
				activate_mission = ALO_united_alash_campaign
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { has_country_flag = zhanar_faction_banned }
					}
					activate_mission = ALO_janar_campaign
				}	
				if = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { has_country_flag = alash_faction_banned }
					}
					activate_mission = ALO_alash_campaign
				}	
				if = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { has_country_flag = national_faction_banned }
					}
					activate_mission = ALO_nationalist_campaign
				}	
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = alash.999
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.999" }
	title = alash.999.t
	desc = {
		text = alash.999.d
		trigger = { ALO_alash_party_in_power = yes }
	}
	desc = {
		text = alash.999.d2
		trigger = { ALO_alash_party_in_power = no }
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = { 
			has_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_ended
			has_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_secured
			has_country_flag = ALO_azat_party_established
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_ALO_azat
	
	option = {
		name = alash.999.a
		trigger = { ALO_alash_party_in_power = yes }
		set_country_flag = ALO_azat_party_established
		clr_country_flag = ALO_1936_Dosmukhamedov_Dulatov
		set_country_flag = ALO_1936_Dosmukhamedov_Socdem
		hidden_effect = {
			1212 = {
				add_to_variable = { ALO_state_azat_pop = ALO_state_zhas_azamat_pop }
				set_variable = { ALO_state_zhas_azamat_pop = 0 }
				add_to_variable = { ALO_state_azat_temp_pop = ALO_state_zhas_azamat_temp_pop }
				set_variable = { ALO_state_zhas_azamat_temp_pop = 0 }
				ALO_get_final_popularities = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			set_temp_variable = { azat_pop = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { zhas_azamat_pop = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { state = 1212 }
				ALO_azat_pop = yes
			}
			else = {
				ALO_zhas_azamat_pop = yes 
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = -0.06
		}
		ALO_bop_yermekov_medium = yes		
		set_temp_variable = { party_support = ALO_azat_deputies }
		multiply_temp_variable = { party_support = -1 }
		ALO_change_azat_support = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = ALO_Khalel_Dosmuhamedov_for_sli }
			remove_ideas = ALO_Khalel_Dosmuhamedov_for_sli
			if = {
				limit = { ALO_yermekov_in_power = yes }
				add_ideas = ALO_Aydarkhan_Turlybaev_for_mli
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ALO_dulatov_in_power = yes }
				add_ideas = ALO_Ahmet_Beremzhanov_for_sli
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				ALO_alash_right_independent = yes
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = zhanar_faction_banned
					has_country_flag = alash_faction_banned
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_secured	
			set_country_flag = azat_faction_banned
			set_country_flag = national_faction_banned
			KAZ = {			
				set_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_secured	
				set_country_flag = azat_faction_banned
				set_country_flag = national_faction_banned
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = ALO_wounds_of_alash }
				remove_ideas = ALO_wounds_of_alash
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ALO_modernization_dynamic_modifier } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = ALO_modernization_remove_pp_cost
				set_variable = { ALO_modernization_political_power_cost = 0 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ORE = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = market_liberal
					name = ALO_social_liberal_party2
					long_name = ALO_social_liberal_party2_long
				}
			}
			URL = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_democrat
					name = ALO_socdem_party
					long_name = ALO_socdem_party_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_liberal
					name = ALO_socdem_party
					long_name = ALO_socdem_party_long
				}
			}
		}		
	}
	option = {
		name = alash.999.b
		trigger = { ALO_alash_party_in_power = no }
		set_country_flag = ALO_azat_party_established
		every_owned_state = {
			set_temp_variable = { azat_pop = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { zhas_azamat_pop = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { state = 1212 }
				ALO_azat_pop = yes
			}
			else = {
				ALO_zhas_azamat_pop = yes 
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = -0.06
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				ALO_alash_right_independent = yes
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = zhanar_faction_banned
					has_country_flag = alash_faction_banned
				}
			}

		NOT = { 
			has_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_ended
			has_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_secured
		}
	}

		name = alash.1287.a
		set_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_secured

		set_country_flag = ALO_bop_ended
		hidden_effect = {
			KAZ = { set_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_secured }
			set_country_flag = zhanar_faction_banned
			set_country_flag = azat_faction_banned
			set_country_flag = national_faction_banned
			every_owned_state = {
				ALO_get_final_popularities = yes
				add_to_variable = { ALO_state_alash_pop = ALO_state_zhanar_pop }
				set_variable = { ALO_state_zhanar_pop = 0 }
				set_variable = { ALO_state_zhanar_temp_pop = 0 }
				if = {
					limit = { 
						ROOT = { ALO_alash_right_independent = no }
					}
					add_to_variable = { ALO_state_alash_pop = ALO_state_national_pop }
					set_variable = { ALO_state_national_pop = 0 }
					set_variable = { ALO_state_national_temp_pop = 0 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						ROOT = { ALO_alash_left_independent = no }
					}
					add_to_variable = { ALO_state_alash_pop = ALO_state_azat_pop }
					set_variable = { ALO_state_azat_pop = 0 }
					set_variable = { ALO_state_azat_temp_pop = 0 }
				}
				ALO_set_new_popularities_after_election = yes
			}
			# Parliament #
			add_to_variable = { ALO_alash_deputies = ALO_zhanar_deputies }
			set_variable = { ALO_zhanar_deputies = 0 }
			set_variable = { ALO_zhanar_deputies_support = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { ALO_alash_right_independent = no }
				}
				add_to_variable = { ALO_alash_deputies = ALO_national_deputies }
				set_variable = { ALO_national_deputies = 0 }
				set_variable = { ALO_national_deputies_support = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { ALO_alash_left_independent = no }
				}
				add_to_variable = { ALO_alash_deputies = ALO_azat_deputies }
				set_variable = { ALO_azat_deputies = 0 }
				set_variable = { ALO_azat_deputies_support = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ALO_alash_right_independent = no }
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					name = ALO_market_liberal_party
					long_name = ALO_alash_party_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					name = ALO_market_liberal_party
					long_name = ALO_alash_party_long
				}
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				name = ALO_market_liberal_party
				long_name = ALO_alash_party_long
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				name = ALO_market_liberal_party
				long_name = ALO_alash_party_long
			}
		}
		ALO_calculate_support = yes

			limit = {
				check_variable = { ALO_alash_deputies > ALO_total_support }

					has_country_flag = ALO_jas_azamat_ally_azat

country_event = {
	id = alash.1269
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.1269" }
	title = alash.1269.t
	desc = alash.1269.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_ALO_khan_elections
	trigger = {
		tag = ALO
		has_liberal_government = yes
		ALO_is_monarchy = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = alash.1269.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = TRK_khanate }
			set_cosmetic_tag = ALO_turkestan
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = ALO_khanate }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = ALO_declared_independence }
					ALO_has_russian_influence = yes
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = ALO_autonomy
			}
			else = {
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					has_cosmetic_tag = ALO_kazakhstan_khanate 
					has_cosmetic_tag = ALO_kazakhstan_khanate_national_social 
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = ALO_declared_independence }
					ALO_has_russian_influence = yes
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = ALO_kazakhstan_autonomy
			}
			else = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = ALO_kazakhstan
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = ALO_khan_namik
					has_country_flag = ALO_khan_orhan
					has_country_flag = ALO_khan_abdulkerim
				}
			}
			TUR = { country_event = alash.1268 }
		}
		effect_tooltip = { retire_ideology_leader = authoritarian_democrat }
		hidden_effect = {
			retire_ideology_leader = social_conservative
			retire_ideology_leader = authoritarian_democrat
			retire_ideology_leader = paternal_autocrat
		}
	}	
}

				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = social_conservative }

			ALO_change_alash_support = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { party_support = 5 }
			ALO_change_national_support = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_support = -3 }
			ALO_change_azat_support = yes
		}
		remove_ideas_with_trait = economy_minister
		add_ideas = ALO_Mukhamedjan_Tynyshpayev_eco_sli
		set_temp_variable = { ALO_loyalty_change = -1 }
		ALO_change_azat_loyalty = yes
		set_temp_variable = { ALO_loyalty_change = 2 }
		ALO_change_national_loyalty = yes			
		set_temp_variable = { ruling_party_pop = -10 }
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = { state = 589 }
			ALO_ruling_party_pop = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = { decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes }
	}
	option = {
		name = alash.798.a
		trigger = { has_government = social_conservative }
		set_temp_variable = { national_pop = 5 }
		every_owned_state = {
			ALO_national_pop = yes
		}	
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { party_support = -3 }
		ALO_change_azat_support = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_support = 5 }
		ALO_change_national_support = yes
		remove_ideas_with_trait = economy_minister
		add_ideas = ALO_Mukhamedjan_Tynyshpayev_eco_sli

				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = ALO_autonomy }
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = ALO_autonomy
			}
		}
	}

				name = "Äzimhan"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/ALO/Portrait_ALO_Azimkhan_Kenesarin.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = junta_subtype
			}
		}		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = ush_zhus_banned }			
			ALO_setup_monarch_for_natpop_slot = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = ALO_Truth_in_Qadimism }
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = social_conservative }
				set_country_leader_ideology = qadhimism_subtype
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
				set_country_leader_ideology = authdem_qadhimism_subtype
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
				set_country_leader_ideology = pataut_qadhimism_subtype
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = ALO_Steppe_Democracy }
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = social_conservative }
				set_country_leader_ideology = soccon_generic_national_democracy_subtype
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
				set_country_leader_ideology = generic_national_democracy_subtype 
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = ALO_turkestan }
			set_cosmetic_tag = TRK_khanate
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = ALO_kazakhstan }
			set_cosmetic_tag = ALO_kazakhstan_khanate
		}
		else = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = ALO_khanate
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = alash.484
				days = 25
			}
			random_other_country = { news_event = turkestan_news.34 }
		}
	}

country_event = { # Final Liberation
	id = alash.720
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.720" }
	title = alash.720.t
	desc = alash.720.d
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = alash.720.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = ALO_Oppress_Non_Qazaqs
				has_completed_focus = ALO_Peoples_Revolution
				has_completed_focus = ALO_Socialism_Under_Quran
				has_country_flag = ALO_comprehensive_sedentarization_started
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ALO_is_monarchy = yes }
				set_cosmetic_tag = ALO_kazakhstan_khanate_national_social
			}
			else = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = ALO_kazakhstan_national_social
			}
			set_country_flag = ALO_ush_zhus_natpop
			hidden_effect = {
				set_temp_variable = { ALO_new_natpop = party_popularity_100@national_populist }
				add_to_temp_variable = { ALO_new_natpop = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist  }

				set_temp_variable = { sum = 100 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@totalist }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@syndicalist }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_democrat }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_liberal }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@market_liberal }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_conservative }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = ALO_new_natpop }

				add_to_temp_variable = { ALO_new_natpop = sum } #avoid rounding errors

				set_popularities = {
					totalist = party_popularity_100@totalist
					syndicalist = party_popularity_100@syndicalist
					radical_socialist = 0
					social_democrat = party_popularity_100@social_democrat
					social_liberal = party_popularity_100@social_liberal
					market_liberal = party_popularity_100@market_liberal
					social_conservative = party_popularity_100@social_conservative
					authoritarian_democrat = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat
					paternal_autocrat = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat
					national_populist = ALO_new_natpop
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = national_populist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = national_populist
				name = ALO_radical_socialist_party
				long_name = ALO_radical_socialist_party_long
			}
			add_radsoc_to_coalition = yes
			set_country_leader_ideology = natpop_popular_patriotism_subtype
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = { ideology = national_populist popularity = 0.1 }
		}
	}
}

					}
					add_to_variable = { ALO_state_alash_pop = ALO_state_azat_pop }
					set_variable = { ALO_state_azat_pop = 0 }
					set_variable = { ALO_state_azat_temp_pop = 0 }
				}
				ALO_set_new_popularities_after_election = yes
			}
			# Parliament #

			set_variable = { ALO_zhanar_deputies_support = 0 }

				set_variable = { ALO_national_deputies = 0 }

		}

			if = {
				limit = { ALO_yermekov_in_power = yes }
				ALO_bop_yermekov_large = yes

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.53" }
	title = alash.53.t
	desc = alash.53.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = alash.53.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				add = -50
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				has_stability < 0.3
			}
		}				
		ALO = {
			country_event = {
				id = alash.54
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = alash.53.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_war = no
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				has_stability > 0.3
			}
		}				
		ALO = {
			country_event = {
				id = alash.55
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = alash.55
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.55" }
	title = alash.55.t
	desc = alash.55.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = alash.55.a
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_trade_agreement 
		}
		random_list = {
			70 = {
				random_owned_controlled_state = { increase_state_category_by_one_level = yes }
			}
			20 = { 
				add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
			}
			10 = {
				add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}
		
country_event = { #North Kazakhstan
	id = alash.1100
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.1100" }
	title = alash.1100.t
	desc = alash.1100.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes 
	
	option = {
		name = alash.1100.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { 
					region = 221
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = ROOT }
					remove_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				add_to_faction = ROOT
				set_faction_name = "Sino-Turkic Prosperity Sphere"
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = alash.1102
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = alash.1100.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 85
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { default_attack_AI_trigger_FROM = yes }
			}
		}
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_3 = yes
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = alash.1101
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}	
}

	desc = alash.1101.d

country_event = { #North Kazakhstan
	id = alash.1102
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.1102" }
	title = alash.1102.t
	desc = alash.1102.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes 
	
	option = {
		name = alash.1102.a
		every_state = {
			limit = { 
				region = 221
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = ROOT }
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
				set_country_flag = was_in_faction_with_RUS
			}
			FROM = { dismantle_faction = yes }
			add_to_faction = FROM
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = was_in_faction_with_RUS }
				ROOT = { add_to_faction = PREV }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_to_faction = FROM
		}	
		set_faction_name = "Sino-Turkic Prosperity Sphere"			
	}
}
country_event = { #
	id = alash.1110
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.1110" }
	title = alash.1110.t
	desc = alash.1110.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes 
	
	option = {
		name = alash.1110.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					turkestan_is_unaligned = yes
					turkestan_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = no
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 99 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				strength_ratio = { tag = FROM ratio < 1 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = { tag = FROM ratio < 0.75 }
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { 
				is_claim_or_core_of_FROM = yes
			}
			transfer_state_to = FROM
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = alash.1112
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = alash.1110.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01 #so there will be a chance to pick this if path set
				FROM = { enemies_strength_ratio < 1 }
				strength_ratio = { tag = FROM ratio < 0.5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				strength_ratio = { tag = ROOT ratio > 1 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = { tag = ROOT ratio > 1.5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				strength_ratio = { tag = ROOT ratio > 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 199 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 149 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 49 }
			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.05
		FROM = {
			country_event = alash.1111
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #
	id = alash.1112
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.1112" }
	title = alash.1112.t
	desc = alash.1112.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes 
	
	option = {
		name = alash.1112.a
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = medium_increase }
		add_political_power = 25
		every_owned_state = {
			set_temp_variable = { ruling_party_pop = 3 }
			ALO_ruling_party_pop = yes
		}
	}
}
